if (!is_file('ajax.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: ajax.php');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('ajax.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): ajax.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('ajax.php') != 'fd0f7a4115034083143dedbfa73c3867f2ea5336') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): ajax.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('ajax.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of ajax.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('ajax.php') !== 'fd0f7a4115034083143dedbfa73c3867f2ea5336') {
		if (@sha1_file('ajax.php') !== 'f326d618f1db07e5db034338bac122f6c73d5a3f') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: ajax.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('ajax.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('ajax.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('ajax.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('ajax.php') !== 'fd0f7a4115034083143dedbfa73c3867f2ea5336') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): ajax.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('oidplus.css')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: oidplus.css');
	writefile_6();
	if (!is_file('oidplus.css')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): oidplus.css');
	} else if (sha1_file('oidplus.css') != '7cebd71b91289390c355589b91506114b4e27417') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): oidplus.css');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('oidplus.css', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of oidplus.css');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('oidplus.css') !== '7cebd71b91289390c355589b91506114b4e27417') {
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus.css') !== 'd75bd3a3709ebf35cf7074a1f33d8034a9bc17d7') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: oidplus.css');
			$tmp = pathinfo('oidplus.css');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('oidplus.css')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('oidplus.css', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_6();
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus.css') !== '7cebd71b91289390c355589b91506114b4e27417') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): oidplus.css');
		}
	}
}

	} else if (sha1_file('oidplus.js') != 'b3c1cf358c5a4c741e530434e7a61d38cea242b1') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): oidplus.js');

			if (!@copy('oidplus.js', $backup_name)) {

		}

	writefile_19();
	if (!is_file('plugins/publicPages/300_search/plugin.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/publicPages/300_search/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/300_search/plugin.inc.php') != '9f7b1e86d7020273f69b074d4514ef8dfe9b98b0') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/publicPages/300_search/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/publicPages/300_search/plugin.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/publicPages/300_search/plugin.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/300_search/plugin.inc.php') !== '9f7b1e86d7020273f69b074d4514ef8dfe9b98b0') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/300_search/plugin.inc.php') !== 'f6e5710a29afa328bad382af03bc17c9b2e7e284') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/publicPages/300_search/plugin.inc.php');

			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/publicPages/300_search/plugin.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_19();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/300_search/plugin.inc.php') !== '9f7b1e86d7020273f69b074d4514ef8dfe9b98b0') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/publicPages/300_search/plugin.inc.php');

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/raPages/101_change_password/plugin.inc.php');
	writefile_24();
	if (!is_file('plugins/raPages/101_change_password/plugin.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/raPages/101_change_password/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/raPages/101_change_password/plugin.inc.php') != '28c0d867f283fe6ade9fbda2559db8f8918eadd0') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/raPages/101_change_password/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/raPages/101_change_password/plugin.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/raPages/101_change_password/plugin.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/raPages/101_change_password/plugin.inc.php') !== '28c0d867f283fe6ade9fbda2559db8f8918eadd0') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/raPages/101_change_password/plugin.inc.php') !== '7017bb01bb39ef58080df85e7b3cb316b470d195') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/raPages/101_change_password/plugin.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/raPages/101_change_password/plugin.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/raPages/101_change_password/plugin.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/raPages/101_change_password/plugin.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_24();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/raPages/101_change_password/plugin.inc.php') !== '28c0d867f283fe6ade9fbda2559db8f8918eadd0') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/raPages/101_change_password/plugin.inc.php');
		}
	}
}
